oh gn bk">Recently noticed large campaigns spreading Android malware which have been followed by both MalwareHunterTeam and Daniel Lopez[1]. Taking a quick glance at the manifest shows they are definitely packed as some of the manifest is referencing code that doesn’t exist in ‘com.example.myapplicationtest’.</p><p id="64e0" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">To unpack it statically we just need to figure out where the next DEX file is stored at and how to decode it, the first thing I notice is the strings are encoded in sub functions:</p><pre class="oi oj ok ol om on oo op oq ay or bk"><span id="6d3f" class="os ot hj oo b jd ou ov l js condition&#x27;)</span></pre><p id="5181" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">This would take awhile to decode every string from every source code file however so instead we will automate it a bit using regular expressions.</p><pre class="oi oj ok ol om on oo op oq ay or bk"><span id="6021" class="os ot hj oo b jd class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">The bot also has an onboard DGA for generating domains with a hardcoded list of TLDs</p><pre class="oi oj ok ol om on oo op oq ay or bk"><span id="1d37" class="os ot hj oo b jd ou ov l js ow">.ru<br/>.com<br/>.cn</span></pre><p id="2cf9" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">The seed for it is based on the date:</p><pre class="oi oj ok ol om on oo op oq ay or bk"><span id="6ce1" class="os ot hj oo b jd ou ov l js ow">private static void GetSeed() {<br/>        int i = Calendar.getInstance().get(1);<br/>        int i2 = Calendar.getInstance().get(2);<br/>        long j = (long) ((i ^ i2) ^ 0);<br/>        seed = j;<br/>        j *= 2;<br/>        seed = j;<br/>        j *= ((long) i) ^ j;<br/>        seed = j;<br/>        long j2 = (((long) i2) ^ j) * j;<br/>        seed = j2;<br/>        j2 *= ((long) 0) ^ j2;<br/>        seed = j2;<br/>        seed = j2 + 1136;<br/>    }</span></pre><p id="7518" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">The first will be the year and the second value will be the month, remebering that java calendar starts counting the months at 0.</p><p id="e8dc" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">We can do the same trick we used for decoding the strings by just reusing the code at hand and changing it up a bit to generate all available domains and dump them out:</p><pre class="oi oj ok ol om on oo op oq ay or bk"><span id="a368" class="os ot hj oo b jd ou ov l js ow">import java.util.Calendar;<br/>import java.util.Random;</span><span id="0b31" class="os ot hj oo b jd ox ov l js ow">public class myTest {<br/>    private static long seed;<br/>    private static final int MAX_HOSTS = 2000;</span><span id="efba" class="os ot hj oo b jd ox ov l js ow">private static void GetSeed() {<br/>        int i = Calendar.getInstance().get(1);<br/>        int i2 = Calendar.getInstance().get(2);<br/>        long j = (long) ((i ^ i2) ^ 0);<br/>        seed = j;<br/>        j *= 2;<br/>        seed = j;<br/>        j *= ((long) i) ^ j;<br/>        seed = j;<br/>        long j2 = (((long) i2) ^ j) * j;<br/>        seed = j2;<br/>        j2 *= ((long) 0) ^ j2;<br/>        seed = j2;<br/>        seed = j2 + 1136;<br/>    }</span><span id="f32a" class="os ot hj oo b jd ox ov l js ow">public static void main(String[] args) {<br/>  GetSeed();<br/>        Random random = new Random(seed);<br/>  for (int i = 0; i &lt; MAX_HOSTS; i++) {<br/>            String string = &quot;&quot;;<br/>            for (int i2 = 0; i2 &lt; 15; i2++) {<br/>                string = string + ((char) (random.nextInt(25) + 97));<br/>            }<br/>   String r1 = i % 3 == 0 ? string + &quot;.ru&quot; : i % 2 == 0 ? string + &quot;.com&quot; : string + &quot;.cn&quot;;<br/>    System.out.println(r1);<br/>  }<br/>  }<br/>}</span></pre><p id="204f" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk">This will spit out all the domains for this month, if you want a different month just manipulate the i2 variable in the GetSeed function.</p><p id="82e2" class="pw-post-body-paragraph nk nl hj nm b nn no np nq nr ns nt nu nv nw nx ny nz oa ob oc od oe of og oh gn bk"><strong class="nm hk">IOCs</strong></p><p id="8922"
